				<string>LimitKit
********
LimitKit is an event logging system and rate limiting tool for shortcuts.

Shortcut developers can use LimitKit to:

1. Track and log events made in shortcuts.
2. Rate limit shortcut operations by calculating whether a set amount of time has elapsed since the last successful log event.

LimitKit works especially well with Autocuts, the solution for running shortcuts automatically in the background while you use your iOS 13 device by allowing background shortcuts to limit their run frequency by seconds, minutes, hours, days, weeks, months, or even years.

https://adamtow.github.io/autocuts</string>
